 How to prepare for UPSC
 
 - Make complete understanding of syllabus
 
 
 UPSC ke pariksha strecchar ko samajhnaa bahut jaruri he

 Paracetamol is generally considered safe to use during pregnancy as a fever or pain reliever, but a recent research has shown that taking paracetamol in pregnancy has an effect on the sexuality of the fetus and also makes it aggressive
 gives
 denmark ke copenhagen vishvavidhyalay ke ek nae shodh main paracetamol ke istemaal se pehle kai baar sochane kii salaah di gai he
 This research has been published in the journal Reproduction
 isamen jaanavar par kiye gaye shodh main lokapriy dardanivarak paracetamol ke istemaal ko purush vyavhaar ke vikaas ke liye nuksaandeh paaya gaya he
 Researchers have said that the dose given to the rat was almost equal to the dose given to a pregnant woman
 haalanki, shodhakartaaon kaa kahana he ki yah prayog sirf chuhon tak simit rahaa, isliye ise sidhe taur par maanav par lagu nahin kiya ja saktaa
 During the research, David Mobjerg Kritensen, who was associated with the University of Copenhagen, said that it would be inappropriate for researchers to test it on humans because of the certainty of the harmful effects of paracetamol
 france main anvyrement at trowell (iaresaiti) va ab institute di richerche in cente se jude mobajarg critensen ne kaha, "ek pareekshan main paracetamol die gaye chuuhe hamaare dwaara niyantrit kiye gaye chuhon kii tarah sambhog karne main saadhaaran taur par aksham rahe
 The male system did not develop properly during embryonic development, and this can be seen in their later adult life
 yah chintajanak he
 "comments mosberg christensen ne kaha ki pehle ke shodh main dekha gaya he ki paracetamol ke istemaal se nar bhrunon main testostoron sex hormone kaa vikaas baadhit hota he
 This increases the risk of testicular deformity in infants, but low levels of testosterone in the fetal stage are also important for the behavior of older men

 ) is shodh kaa prakaashan patrika 'riproduction' main kiya gaya he
 In this, research on animals has found the use of the popular analgesic paracetamol to be harmful for the development of male behavior

 shodh ke dauraan copenhegan vishvavidhyalay se jude rahe david mobajarg critensen ne kaha ki shodhakartaaon dwaara paracetamol ke hanikaarak prabhaav kii nischitata kii vajah se iskaa pareekshan maanav par kiya janaa anuchit hoga
 Möbjerg Kritensen, associated with the Environment at Trouvel (IRSET) in France and now the Institut de Richerche in Sante, said, "in a trial, rats given paracetamol were simply unable to orgasm like the rats we controlled

 Because the Parliamentary Secretary in Delhi can be in the Chief Minister's office, not the ministers
 yahi kanoon chunaav ayog kii internal report main kejariwal ke sansadeey sachivon ke liye musiibat ban rahaa he or 21 vidhayakon kii sadsyta bhi khatre main hai
 Read what the law says here: 1
 dilli ke kanoon main likhaa he kisansadeey sachivho saktaa he, lekin mukhyamantri ke offis ko ye adhikaar he
 There is no provision of Parliamentary Secretary in the rest of the ministers' offices
 2
 The Kejriwal government added to the bill that the Parliamentary Secretary can be with the Chief Minister as well as the Minister
 3
 Delhi can have 10 per cent ministers, if it makes 21 parliamentary secretaries, it would be against the constitution
 4
 In 1997, in a bill passed to remove a disqualification, only two offices were allowed on the ground of 'office of profit', this exemption was given to the chairman of a Khadiboard and the chairman of another women's committee
 5
 After the amendment made in 2006, the Chief Minister has the right to have a Parliamentary Secretary but the Ministers do not have this right
 6
 The Kejriwal government, along with the new amendment, sent a draft to the President to give the ministers the right to have a parliamentary secretary
 lekin raashtrapati ne ise khaarij kar diya
 So this law could not be made
 7
 There are special provisions for the NCT Act in section 192 of the Constitution
 agar koi offis of profit hold karata he to wo vidhansabha se apni sadsyta kho saktaa he
 Now the President will step in following the Election Commission's opinion in this matter
 agar wo samvidhan ke hisaab se kaam karenge to 21 sansadeey sachiv apni sadsyta kho denge or phir dobaaraa chunaav honge
 8
 kai rajyon main mantriyon ne bhi sansadeey sachiv rakhe hue hai, lekin isaki manjuuri milane or kanoon banane ke baad aisa hua he
 But before the approval of the Delhi government, the Parliamentary Secretary was appointed and due to the non-enactment of the law, his membership is now non-parliamentary and illegal
 9
 Governments in many states also challenged this in the High Court
 lekin court ne yachika ko khaarij kar diya

 sadsyta radd hone or dobaaraa chunaav hone me kitna samay lagegaa ye nirvachan ayog ke vivek par he
